***boer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a> (3550)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*būr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*būraz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dweller, inhabitant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thus originally the same as modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:buur.html>buur</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">neighbour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form <i><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that of many eastern dialects including <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limburgish" class="extiw" title="w:Limburgish">Limburgish</a></span>, where Germanic <i>-ū-</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> retained as a back vowel. In early modern Dutch these two dialectal forms <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> adopted as semantically distinguished <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">būr</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ġebūr</i> (whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bower.html>bower</a></i>) and Old High German <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">būr</i> (whence German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bauer</i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boertje.html>boertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerin.html>boerin</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>(male) farmer, peasant
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bouwman</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:landbouwer.html>landbouwer</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">teler</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tuinder.html>tuinder</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:veehouder.html>veehouder</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in compounds</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> merchant (and sometimes producer) of a certain product group, mainly foods, often named after it, e.g. <a href = vnd.unilang:melkboer.html>melkboer</a> 'milkman', <a href = vnd.unilang:groenteboer.html>groenteboer</a> '(male) greengrocer'</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:boor.html>boor</a>, yokel, ruffian</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:jack.html>jack</a> (playing card)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally onomatopoetic, as <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">burp</i>. The perception of farmers (etymology 1) as being mannerless people <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> probably played a secondary role, too. The same in German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Bäuerchen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boer.html>boer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boertje.html>boertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A belch, a burp.</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeren.html>boeren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to farm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erij</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">place associated with an activity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with the interfixed <i>-d-</i> originally being a dialectal element.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerderij.html>boerderij</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerderijen.html>boerderijen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boerderijtje.html>boerderijtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">farm</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boete.html>boete</a> (5207)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boete.html>boete</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bōta</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōtō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">recompense</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boten.html>bote</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">profit, plunder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***boeten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boeten.html>boeten</a> (2888)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeten.html>boeten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to improve</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*buoten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōtijaną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boeten.html>boeten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pay for something as punishment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to expiate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:boeten.html>boeten</a></b>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">boutique</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Occitan" class="extiw" title="w:Old Occitan">Old Occitan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pro">botica</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">apothēca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀποθήκη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apothḗkē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">boetse</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a sketch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bozza</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a draft</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boesem</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bōsmaz</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boezem.html>boezem</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boezems.html>boezems</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boezem.html>boezempje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">bosom</span>
<ol><li>human chest (regardless of gender)</li>
<li>female breasts</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> as the seat of emotion</li></ol></li>
<li>body of water without a fully controlled water level, used for collecting water pumped out of polders before it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> discharged into a major river or sea.</li>

***boggle.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a> (84649)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variation or derivation of bogle, possibly cognate with bug
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">boggles</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boggling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boggled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive or intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Either literally or figuratively to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> or hesitate as if suddenly seeing a bogle.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The dogs <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> on, but the horse <b>boggled</b> at the sudden appearance of the strange beast.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The horror of the <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> and its consequences <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> the imagination.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><dl><dd>Do by thy soul, when thou findest it shy of such meditations, as <a href = vnd.unilang:wee.html>wee</a> do by our <a href = vnd.unilang:horses.html>horses</a>, that are given to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> and start when <a href = vnd.unilang:wee.html>wee</a> ride them; When they fly back, and start at anything in the way, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> do not yield to their fear, and go back (that will make them worse another time) but <a href = vnd.unilang:wee.html>wee</a> ride them up close to that they are afraid of, and so in time break them of that ill quality. <sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be bewildered, dumbfounded, or confused.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">He <b>boggled</b> at the surprising news.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The mind <b>boggles</b>.</i></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1661</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Glanvill" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph Glanvill">Joseph Glanvill</a>, <i>The Vanity of Dogmatizing</i>, London: <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Eversden, Chapter 14, p. 131,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A42833.0001.001">[2]</a></sup>
<dl><dd><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> start and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> at what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i>unusual</i>: and like the <i>Fox</i> in the fable at his first view of the <i>Lyon</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> cannot endure the sight of the <i>Bug-bear</i>, <i>Novelty</i>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1685</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Isaac_Barrow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Isaac Barrow">Isaac Barrow</a>, <i>Of Contentment, Patience and Resignation to the Will of <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a>. Several Sermons</i>, London: Brabazon Aylmer, Sermon 4, pp. 127-128,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A31073.0001.001">[3]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>They are <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> qualified to thrive in [this world] <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> whose <a href = vnd.unilang:designs.html>designs</a> all tend to their own private advantage, without any regard to the publick, or to the good of others; who can use any means conducible to such <a href = vnd.unilang:designs.html>designs</a>, <b>bogling</b> at nothing which serveth their purpose <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1795</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Wollstonecraft" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mary Wollstonecraft"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Wollstonecraft</a>, letter to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gilbert_Imlay" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Gilbert Imlay"><a href = vnd.unilang:gilbert.html>Gilbert</a> Imlay</a> dated 4 October, 1795, in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Wollstonecraft: <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a> to Imlay</i>, London: Kegan Paul, 1879, p. 182,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/letterstoimlaywi00wolluoft">[4]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>From the tenour of your last letter however, I am <a href = vnd.unilang:led.html>led</a> to imagine, that you have formed some new attachment.—If it be so, let <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> earnestly request you to see <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> once more, and immediately. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the only proof I require of the friendship you profess for <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>. I will then decide, since you <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> about a mere form.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1969</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Maya_Angelou" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Maya Angelou"><a href = vnd.unilang:maya.html>Maya</a> Angelou</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/I_Know_Why_the_Caged_Bird_Sings" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:I Know Why the Caged Bird Sings">I Know Why the Caged Bird <a href = vnd.unilang:sings.html>Sings</a></a></i>, New York: Bantam, 1971, Chapter 15, p. 82,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/iknowwhycagedbi000maya">[5]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>My imagination <b>boggled</b> at the punishment I would deserve <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To confuse or mystify; overwhelm.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The vastness of space really <b>boggles</b> the mind.</i></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The oddities of quantum <a href = vnd.unilang:mechanics.html>mechanics</a> can <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> the <a href = vnd.unilang:minds.html>minds</a> of students and experienced physicists alike.</i></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To embarrass with difficulties; to palter or equivocate; to bungle or botch.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To dissemble; to play fast and loose (<i>with</i> someone or something).
<ul><li><b>1643</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Howell" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:James Howell">James Howell</a>, <i>The True Informer</i>, London, p. 32,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A44760.0001.001">[6]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>I would be loth to exchange consciences with them, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></b> so with <a href = vnd.unilang:god.html>God</a> Almighty; but these <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> by a new <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <i>Metaphysick</i> have found out a way to abstract the <i>Person</i> of the King from his Office to make his Soveraigntie a kinde of <i>Platonick Idea</i> hovering in the aire, while they visibly attempt to assail and destroy his person <span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boggle.html>boggle</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">boggles</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A scruple or objection.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bungle; a botched situation.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bogle</i></span></span></li></ol>

***boilers.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boilers.html>boilers</a> (76930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boilers.html>boilers</a></strong>
</p>

***bois.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bois.html>bois</a> (95012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:bois.html>bois</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">boys</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">boiz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bosc, <a href = vnd.unilang:bois.html>bois</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">boscus</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*buscus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*busk</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*buskaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bush, thicket</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:bosco.html>bosco</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">bosque</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bos.html>bos</a></i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bush</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>wood (material)</li>
<li>wood, woodland</li>
<li>antler</li>
<li>woodwind</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boksbal.html>boksbal</a> (30675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***bol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a> (4802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bolle.html>bolle</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*bolla</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bullǭ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">round object or vessel, ball, bowl</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bollen.html>bollen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bolletje.html>bolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bolleke.html>bolleke</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ball, sphere, globe, bulb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A head; brain</li>
<li>A scoop (of ice etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mainly the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A large, round spot, dot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">heraldry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> roundel
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koek.html>koek</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A bun, a roll, a round piece of bread or pastry.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boller.html>boller</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">bolst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>convex; bulging</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:chubby.html>chubby</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bollen.html>bollen</a> (20137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bol.html>bol</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bollen.html>bollen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swell, to billow</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to puff out</li></ol>

<p>Generally regarded as borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Judaeo-Spanish" class="extiw" title="w:Judaeo-Spanish">Ladino</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">bollo</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:bola.html>bola</a></i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***bom.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a> (1333)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bombe</i>, still attested as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bombe</i> in Early Modern Dutch.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommen.html>bommen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommetje.html>bommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>bomb <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">explosive</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Surinam</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gas cylinder <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">cylindrical vessel for compressed gas</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">gascylinder</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gasfles.html>gasfles</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Clipping of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bomschuit</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommen.html>bommen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommetje.html>bommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> flat-bottomed marine fishing vessel</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bomme</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bonne.html>bonne</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_6">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommen.html>bommen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bommetje.html>bommetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bung</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:stopper.html>stopper</a></span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">for <a href = vnd.unilang:barrels.html>barrels</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>

***bomaanslag.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bomaanslag.html>bomaanslag</a> (14269)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bom.html>bom</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:aanslag.html>aanslag</a></i>.
</p>

***bombarderen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bombarderen.html>bombarderen</a> (7655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">bombarder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bombarderen.html>bombarderen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bomb, to bombard (to attack with bombs)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bombard figuratively, to overload</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***bonanza.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bonanza.html>bonanza</a> (49857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:bonanza.html>bonanza</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">calm sea, fair weather, good luck, rich lode</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bonacia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fair weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a blend of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">bonus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">good</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">malacia</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">calm sea</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bonanza.html>bonanza</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bonanzas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A rich mine or vein of silver or gold.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">borrasca</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>The point at which two mother lodes intersect.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Anything which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a mine of wealth or yields a large income or return.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">mother lode</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2013</b> August 31,  Bagehot,  “<a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.economist.com/http://www.economist.com/news/britain/21584322-devastation-fishery-shows-idiocy-much-environmental-politics-parable">The parable of the Clyde</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Economist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Economist">The Economist</a></cite>, volume 408, number 8851:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">For two decades the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bonanza.html>bonanza</a></b> on Scotland’s west coast continued. An occupation that <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> seasonal and modestly profitable became year-round and lucrative. <a href = vnd.unilang:baskets.html>Baskets</a> of herring put televisions into fishermen’s <a href = vnd.unilang:cottages.html>cottages</a> and cars outside their <a href = vnd.unilang:doors.html>doors</a>. But fish, like oil and gas, with which Scotland’s continental shelf <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also well-endowed, are not in unlimited supply.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">The popular show quickly became a ratings <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bonanza.html>bonanza</a></b> for the network.</i></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>
